  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_88a0fd61-5d3f-48c1-85fb-ddaa3ebb26f3'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

  <span id="freeText392553783648556788" style="display:none">Tessa and Hardin have defied all the odds, but will their fairy tale ending be turned on its head? AFTER EVER HAPPY...Life will never be the same. #HESSA<br /><br />It’s never been all rainbows and sunshine for Tessa and Hardin, but each new challenge they’ve faced has only made their passionate bond stronger and stronger. But when a revelation about the past shakes Hardin’s inpenetrable façade to the core—and then Tessa suffers a tragedy—will they stick together again, or be torn apart?<br /><br />As the shocking truth about each of their families emerges, it’s clear the two lovers are not so different from each other. Tessa is no longer the sweet, simple, good girl she was when she met Hardin—any more than he is the cruel, moody boy she fell so hard for. Tessa understands all the troubling emotions brewing beneath Hardin’s exterior, and she knows she’s the only one who can calm him when he erupts. He needs her.<br /><br />But the more layers of his past come to light, the darker he grows, and the harder he pushes Tessa—and everyone else in his life—away. Tessa’s not sure if she really can save him—not without sacrificing herself. She refuses to go down without a fight. But who is she fighting for—Hardin or herself?</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1300428736" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3124350149100144307">I never in a million years thought I would be saying this... I actually really enjoyed this book. I know I know, after how much crap I gave the first three how could this happen. I can't even fully comprehend it myself. As much as I hated this series, this last book won me over. At first I thought that this series was ridiculous but after powering through it I actually completely understand it's madness. For example: I didn't understand why each book need to be 600+ pages, but now I do. This ser</span>
  <span id="freeText3124350149100144307" style="display:none">I never in a million years thought I would be saying this... I actually really enjoyed this book. I know I know, after how much crap I gave the first three how could this happen. I can't even fully comprehend it myself. As much as I hated this series, this last book won me over. At first I thought that this series was ridiculous but after powering through it I actually completely understand it's madness. For example: I didn't understand why each book need to be 600+ pages, but now I do. This series is only written to be over a span of months, but instead of trying to cram all this into 200 pages she decided to just go balls to the wall and make the books as long as they needed to be. You (at least I ended up) feeling like I was going through everything with these characters. Characters that, and I quote, "<i>I would never end up rooting for</i>". Well guess what, I ended up doing just that. I was praying that Tessa and Hardin would end up together. I was hoping that even though everything they went through was so exaggerated, so overdone, far fetched, so pointless that it wouldn't end up being pointless.<br><br>Hardin and Tessa both turned out to be characters I ended up liking. I have <u>
  <b>
    <i>NO CLUE</i>
  </b>
</u> when my opinion of Tessa changed, but I know that it was the middle of the third when Hardin finally made sense. It came out of nowhere too. I was just reading along minding my own business and WHAM, all of a sudden I found myself thinking "<i>Huh, wow I finally get Hardin... I get all his rash decisions, his outburst, and how his attitude is zero dark crazy." </i>Then I found myself saying "<i>What the HELL did I just say?!?"</i><br><br><div>
  <br>
  <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-WJFBlxfzs7w/VXOZMQ42PrI/AAAAAAAABy8/GTjC5uxsRFs/s1600/wthhh.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img height="170" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1433642208ra/15125275.gif" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</div><br><br>Both the writing style and character development in this final book is both leaps and bounds above the other three. Both Hardin and Tessa reached me on a level they never had in the previous books. <i>After Ever Happy, </i>like the others in this series, still had a crazy cluster of a storyline, was still covered in flaws, and still had no real structure to it. I can without a doubt say that the <i>After Series </i>is one of the most pointless things I've ever read, yet I have no regrets about how addicted I was too it. <i>AEH </i>had me laughing, had me on the edge of my seat, and even had me shedding a few tears... Yeah I might have cringed a little too hearing myself saying that, but hell I just read close to 3000 pages of one direction based fanfiction, what do I really have left to be embarrassed about... So I'll say it again; <b>a few tears were shed while reading this! Get off my case! Jeez. </b><br><br>I think the thing that <i>AEH </i>had going for it was that of all four it was the "most realistic". With more touching and real topics happening through out, and more human reactions were given in response to each issue. The<i> After Series </i>turned out to be one of the biggest surprises I've had in my reading history. I completely agree with both negative and positive comment, statement, and review ever written about it, because it is everything everyone has ever said about it. It's annoying, unhealthy, romantic, comical, addictive, and so much more... But damn it if I didn't fall for it even though for some reason I still can't stand it. I still can't manage to figure out what happened to me or when my opinion changed... But Anna Todd I'm pretty sure you've won me over... Maybe, I truly don't full know.<br><br><div>
  <br>
  <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-N9iYSYZ8ecU/VXOgNa3uttI/AAAAAAAABzU/YKvQz02YEVU/s1600/wthhhhhh.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img height="179" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1433642208ra/15125276.gif" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</div><br><br>If it wasn't for the last half of the epilogue I might have given this book a higher rating, but sadly something about the last few pages rubbed me the wrong way. But, I guess all terribly good guilty pleasure reads must come to some kind of end, and I was overall happy with this one.<br><br>Turn on the TV for background noise, grab a jar of peanut butter, and make yourself comfortable, because once you grab a hold of this series you'll be in for the long haul.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3124350149100144307" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2062516600" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2062516600" />
    <a title="Candace" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16384209-candace"><img alt="Candace" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459720769p2/16384209.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2062516600?book_show_action=true">Jul 17, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Candace" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Candace" href="/user/show/16384209-candace">Candace</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/23665391-after-ever-happy">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=listened-to-audio-version">listened-to-audio-version</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=hate-that-i-love-them">hate-that-i-love-them</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2062516600" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5165694089708726835">The fourth book in the 'After' series, 'After Ever Happy' is the first book in the series that had a different "feel" to it. Don't get me wrong, there is plenty of dramatic shenanigans between Tessa and Hardin. However, this time around they aren't the sole focus of the book. The result is a much more somber vibe.<br/><br/>After everything that went down at the end of the third book, Tessa is left markedly changed from the girl she was before. Those tragic events forced her to take a long, hard look at he</span>
  <span id="freeText5165694089708726835" style="display:none">The fourth book in the 'After' series, 'After Ever Happy' is the first book in the series that had a different "feel" to it. Don't get me wrong, there is plenty of dramatic shenanigans between Tessa and Hardin. However, this time around they aren't the sole focus of the book. The result is a much more somber vibe.<br /><br />After everything that went down at the end of the third book, Tessa is left markedly changed from the girl she was before. Those tragic events forced her to take a long, hard look at her relationship with Hardin. She finally faces the facts -- they're toxic.<br /><br />Despite her love for Hardin, she knows that she needs to get away from him. Like the clichéd saying, "sometimes love isn't enough". Nothing could be more true for this dysfunctional couple at that point in time.<br /><br />Even though Hardin comes to his senses and does his best to get Tessa to forgive him, it won't come easy this time around. Tessa has made up her mind and it will take years for Hardin to prove himself to her. It was long overdue.<br /><br />With Tessa and Hardin living separate lives for most of this book, the story definitely had a different feel to it than earlier books. As much as it was what the logical me said needed to happen, the illogical part of me couldn't help but feel like this new direction wasn't as captivating. After all, this series' entire guilty pleasure appeal was based on the very same things that made this couple such a train wreck -- fighting, angst, jealousy, breaking up and making up. With those elements largely missing from this book, I didn't feel the same pull to the story.<br /><br />That being said, I think that the author had used up all of the major angst-ridden story elements that readers could handle. Although the loss of this drama resulted in a slightly less engaging story for me, I don't think I could've handled another book full of Tessa and Hardin's back and forth fighting. This series has left me emotionally exhausted and I just don't have it in me.<br /><br />Luckily, Tessa and Hardin do get the HEA eventually. It was long overdue and I was glad to see it. Finally, they have started to mature and deal with some of the issues in their relationship. As much as I loved to hate this couple, I have to admit that if there was ever a couple that stuck it out, it was them. Talk about hanging in there for better or worse.<br /><br />Overall, this was still a great read. I have been completely hooked on Tessa and Hardin's story right from the start. It was one hell of an emotional rollercoaster ride. I feel content, but emotionally drained. I know that there are two remaining books in this series, but I'm stopping with this one for now. I don't want to upset the balance. I'm feeling content with how this book ended and I'm not sure I could handle it right now if something disrupted that peace.<br /><br />Check out more of my reviews at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.bookaddicthaven.com">www.bookaddicthaven.com</a> </span>
  <a data-text-id="5165694089708726835" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2000467437" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5584475492750120250"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1501010585i/23408076._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1495397230ra/22813206.gif' width='420' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1501010585ra/23408080.gif' width='420' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1501010585ra/23408079.gif' width='420' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1501010585ra/23408078.gif' width='420' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1501010585ra/23408077.gif' width='420' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️1/2! After Ever Happy, book 4 of 5. The conclusion to an against-all-odds romance between tatted rebel Hardin Scott & good girl Tessa Young!</b><br/><br/><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“The fucked-up truth is that people like her are the easiest prey for someone like me, who takes and takes until there is nothing left. That’s what I have done since the beginning, and that’s what I will always do.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br/><u>Books in The After series should be read in order:</u><br/><b>Book 1: <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1090449623' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>After</a><br/>Book 2: <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1952340915' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>After We Collided</a><br/>Book 3: <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1994022284' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>After We Fell</a><br/>Book</b></span>
  <span id="freeText5584475492750120250" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1501010585i/23408076._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1495397230ra/22813206.gif" width="420" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1501010585ra/23408080.gif" width="420" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1501010585ra/23408079.gif" width="420" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1501010585ra/23408078.gif" width="420" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1501010585ra/23408077.gif" width="420" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️1/2! After Ever Happy, book 4 of 5. The conclusion to an against-all-odds romance between tatted rebel Hardin Scott &amp; good girl Tessa Young!</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“The fucked-up truth is that people like her are the easiest prey for someone like me, who takes and takes until there is nothing left. That’s what I have done since the beginning, and that’s what I will always do.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><u>Books in The After series should be read in order:</u><br><b>Book 1: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1090449623" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">After</a><br>Book 2: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1952340915" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">After We Collided</a><br>Book 3: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1994022284" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">After We Fell</a><br>Book 4: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2000467437" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">After Ever Happy</a><br>Book 5: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2000467456" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Before</a></b><br><br>The After series is the epic love saga between flawed rebel bad boy student and editor <b>Hardin Allen Scott</b> and naïve good girl student and intern editor <b>Theresa Lynn Young, Tessa.</b><br><br><i>In <b>After, book 1-3,</b> Tessa met her polar opposite in Hardin. An unlikely friendship blossomed into a <b>dysfunctional and co-dependent love</b> driven by their intense sexual connection.</i><br><br><b>After Ever Happy, book 4</b> is the final chapter in Hardin and Tessa’s saga. Their <b>love will be tested</b> with more revelations, truths and betrayals. But ultimately this is a journey of self-reflection and growth.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1496016874ra/22874859.gif" width="420" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Ten words to describe <b> Hardin Allen Scott:</b> Unpredictable, moody, flawed, aloof, secretive, demanding, conflicted, possessive matured and reflective.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1496016874ra/22874860.gif" width="420" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Ten words to describe <b> Theresa Lynn Young, Tessa:</b> Hard-headed, organized, meek, compulsive, goal-oriented, determined, naïve, trusting, curious and forgiving.<br><br><b>After Ever Happy,</b> told from dual POVs, is an all-consuming, addicting, at times angsty journey of <b>self-discovery, testing boundaries, pushing limits</b> and <b>surrendering</b> it all for love. It ends, though bittersweet to say goodbye, with <b>multiple epilogues</b> following them into their forties.<br><br>***<br>Hero: ★★★★★<br>Heroine: ★★★★<br>Plot: ★★★★<br>Storytelling: ★★★★★<br>Sexual tension: ★★★★<br>Sex scenes: ★★★★★<br>Story ending: ★★★★★+<br>******************************************<br><b>OVERALL RATING:</b> ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️1/2<br>Angst: <b>| MEDIUM FOCUS |</b><br>Darkness: <b>| MEDIUM FOCUS |</b><br>Humor: <b>| LOW FOCUS |</b><br>Kink: <b>| LOW FOCUS |</b><br>Romance: <b>| HIGH FOCUS |</b><br>Sex frequency: <b>| MEDIUM FOCUS |</b><br>Suspense: <b>| MEDIUM FOCUS |</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1501010585ra/23408081.gif" width="420" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1495396964ra/22813189.gif" width="81" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1495397067ra/22813191.gif" width="81" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1495397142ra/22813203.gif" width="81" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1495397230ra/22813206.gif" width="81" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1495397307ra/22813208.gif" width="81" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Thank you</b> to everyone reading &amp; chatting on Shh… Shhurrender your TBR! <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://goo.gl/ccVTB7">https://goo.gl/ccVTB7</a></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13602158412250429096">Caution: Rated R: for language and overall smuttiness <br/>🔥🔥🔥🔥🔥🔥🔥🔥🔥🔥🔥🔥🔥🔥🔥🔥🔥🔥<br/><br/>Alright.... I made it!! 🤗 It was rough- but I made it through all four books. This is the equivalent of binge watching all seasons of Jersey Shore. I’m embarrassed to even admit that I got sucked into this trash world- but I totally did. Each book ‘cliff hanger’ left me needing to read the next one. I couldn’t stop. 🤷🏼‍♀️ Even when I was rolling my eyes and ready to give up, I just had to know what would happen with these tw</span>
  <span id="freeText13602158412250429096" style="display:none">Caution: Rated R: for language and overall smuttiness <br />🔥🔥🔥🔥🔥🔥🔥🔥🔥🔥🔥🔥🔥🔥🔥🔥🔥🔥<br /><br />Alright.... I made it!! 🤗 It was rough- but I made it through all four books. This is the equivalent of binge watching all seasons of Jersey Shore. I’m embarrassed to even admit that I got sucked into this trash world- but I totally did. Each book ‘cliff hanger’ left me needing to read the next one. I couldn’t stop. 🤷🏼‍♀️ Even when I was rolling my eyes and ready to give up, I just had to know what would happen with these two damaged people. <br /><br />Don’t read any further if you’re worried about spoilers:<br /><br />I kinda predicted that Hardin’s dad wasn’t really Kent. They set up a predictable little boy who acted and looked like Hardin- his little brother- of course. Then Hardin lights his moms house on fire?! Goes off the deep end and ditches her in another country?! What happened in the first part of this book was, in my opinion, unforgivable. 🤬😡 She should not have even spoke to him after that.<br /><br />I guess Tessa stood her ground (kinda) and did her own thing away from him (which was kinda good) for a couple years. But this ending had me rolling my eyes. 🙄 Wrapped up in a cute little bow?! I almost feel like it would have been a better ending for them not to have ended up together. 🤔<br /><br />Anyway, I’m moving on from this drama filled series!! Hooray!! I’ve had people ask me why I’d keep reading if it was such a struggle. It’s extremely rare that I don’t finish a book once I start. And as stated, I needed to know how this saga ended. Overall this book is HOT!! 🔥🔥🔥 these types of books are a guilty pleasure of mine and I do read them from time to time. It’s very steamy and if you’re into that kinda read (and have a lot of patience)- I’d definitely recommend this. ❤️📚</span>

<div id="review_1756692533" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1756692533" />
    <a title="Kirsten" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8890968-kirsten"><img alt="Kirsten" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1480426596p2/8890968.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1756692533?book_show_action=true">Sep 19, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kirsten" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kirsten" href="/user/show/8890968-kirsten">Kirsten</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8890968-kirsten?shelf=sweet-2016">sweet-2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8890968-kirsten?shelf=what-did-i-just-read">what-did-i-just-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8890968-kirsten?shelf=teen">teen</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8890968-kirsten?shelf=series">series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1756692533" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4441767212477269541">Well here we are. Literally like, 3,000 pages later and this God-forsaken series is finally over. I know that it still seems like lunacy that I would finish this series even though they're literally worse than garbage, and trust me - I'm scratching my head at this myself. Of all the series for me to decide to ACTUALLY finish, I chose this one? I have no priorities, clearly. But what's done is done, and these books are blessedly in that category.<br/><br/>This whole book was like running uphill - you don't</span>
  <span id="freeText4441767212477269541" style="display:none">Well here we are. Literally like, 3,000 pages later and this God-forsaken series is finally over. I know that it still seems like lunacy that I would finish this series even though they're literally worse than garbage, and trust me - I'm scratching my head at this myself. Of all the series for me to decide to ACTUALLY finish, I chose this one? I have no priorities, clearly. But what's done is done, and these books are blessedly in that category.<br /><br />This whole book was like running uphill - you don't want to do it and you're not sure why you started in the first place but you push on because you feel you have something to prove and even though it was a dumb idea you feel like you accomplished something when you reach the top because it was the worst decision you've made in a while and you clearly didn't look at your life and your choices.<br /><br />You all probably know what types of things I'm going to have to say here, making this review redundant, however I owe it to myself to write down only a handful of the many, MANY reasons this book is worth no one's time and how it actually makes you dumber by reading it. There will be spoilers, and none of you will care because you have higher reading standards and aren't ashamed of yourselves every time you look at your recently read books and see these atrocities listed there. <br /><br />Without further ado, let's bash this book:<br /><br />- How dare Anna Todd spend so much time with two characters who clearly have no intelligent thoughts in their heads? These books were written entirely from within Tessa and Hardin's head, and since neither Hardin or Tessa have enough brain cells to even rub together, there was LITERALLY NOTHING TO TALK ABOUT. Introspection is only a good plot device when characters aren't pieces of crap, and when they're developing as a result of events. Since nothing ever HAPPENS in these books, there's no way for them to be growing and/or changing, so all we get is stagnant crap about souls and poor uses of the "love is a battlefield" metaphor (which was already poor at best, so you can imagine what joys lay in store for me as a reader as I went through this).<br /><br />- #srstalk Tessa's descriptions of depression and mental health kind of offended me. It really seemed to cheapen the seriousness of these issues by being 100% taken from a textbook and/or BuzzFeed article describing symptoms and behaviours. As someone working through their own depression, I was uncomfortable with how casually it was thrown around and was even more mad than usual at this ridiculously stupid girl who needs to get her head out of her own butt and just GROW UP.<br /><br />- Tessa constantly apologized for "not being able to fix" Hardin, making me unsure who I hated more: a girl who clearly has no idea how to be an adult and who always has to make everything about her and everyone's perceptions of her, or a boy who is so destructive to himself and others that there's LITERALLY NO WAY he wouldn't be in jail or forcibly admitted to a hospital of some kind to receive treatment for his mental health and anger issues. Like, they're both so unfathomably unlikable it HURTS<br /><br />- Hardin's only memories of Tessa seem to involve her having sex with him. He literally doesn't seem to have a single fond memory that has anything to do with her as a person or her interests. His only interest is in her body and having sex with it, and if that isn't objectifying women and painting yourself as a chauvinist pig I don't know what is. And Todd seems to think this is a romantic ideal? Grrl, these opinions of men and excusing this type of behaviour is the reason so many women find themselves unable to leave bad relationships because you're telling them this is a good thing. Like ohmylife how can ANYONE even with this book?<br /><br />- It was beyond infuriating to have both Hardin and Tessa constantly making themselves out to be the victim, but especially Hardin. It is always literally 100% his fault. Example: Karen's pregnant and he makes this into a "the world hates me because I'm too fucked up and this is my punishment" thing. WHY CAN'T YOU OWN UP TO EVEN ONE THING AND JUST ADMIT THE WORLD ISN'T COMPLETELY UNFAIR OT YOU AND THAT YOU'RE A RIDICULOUS PERSON?! IT'S NOT ALWAYS ABOUT YOU DICK WAD. ANNA TODD YOU'RE THE WORST BECAUSE NOW I'M YELLING AT FICTIONAL CHARACTERS.<br /><br />- Hardin's idea of compromise is to offer Tessa space only if she'll marry him. The conversation went something like this: "If I give you space that you are entitled to and clearly need because you're deranged, you HAVE to MARRY ME". "Yeah, OK, good trade, good talk, that works for me". What a majestic display of great communication, cooperation, and healthy relationships #lovingthatconcept<br /><br />- Tessa tells Hardin over and over "I need to get away for a while, we spend too much time together and we need a clean break." In the real world, a clean break would mean no contact and "getting away for a while" would probably be a couple of months with you never coming back because that's how normal people tend to heal (there are exceptions, but I'm ignoring them right now for the purposes of being beyond frustrated with these books). In the After universe, "going away for a while" is like, 5 weeks and involves constant contact and lots of random sex as a means of "healing wounds" what even is that. The best part? She tried to make it seem like they were apart for like, 5 years #grrlplz<br /><br />- Hardin proceeds to write a book about their relationship and, surprise surprise, calls it After, and this is where I really lost it. I cannot believe Todd tried to make this book all meta and crap by putting her books inside the books. YOU ARE NOT TALENTED ENOUGH OR INTERESTING ENOUGH FOR THAT. And THEN, on top of THAT, Hardin's book is so immensely popular and all the publishers are fighting for it and everyone wants to read it and are freaking out about it, making this a sad wish fulfillment fantasy a la Twilight and I just got so like, sad because it all just feels so pathetic and I'm rolling my eyes and clutching my face and mumbling "please no, this can't actually be published and available for purchase, what am I doing with my life?" Why can't Todd just write a book that doesn't suck balls and then move on with her life? Harden also describes the book as being about self recovery, and then in the next book tells Tessa they helped each other. How does that even work? If it's self recovery shouldn't you be doing it on your own? WHY DOES NO ONE UNDERSTAND BOOKS IN THIS AFTER UNIVERSE. And Tessa FREAKS OUT about this book even though, for once, Hardin isn't saying ONLY crappy things about her. GRRL YOU ARE SO DUMB I CAN'T.<br /><br />- Nobody speaks the way that Hardin and Tessa speak to each other. Literally no one. It's like they know they have an audience and feel the need to put on a play that no one would be willing to pay for or would even stay halfway through, and then here I am still reading it because I have no self-respect at all. <br /><br />- Hardin became an advocate for self-recovery? Really? Is that even a thing? I'm really just phoning it in at this point, we've moved so far past anything remotely good that it's a struggle to remember this won't be the last book I'll ever read and books aren't actually all garbage.<br /><br />- WHO WAS LANDON'S FIANCEE/WIFE AND WHY DID THEY ALWAYS REFER TO HER SIMPLY AS "LANDON'S BRIDE"? YOU CAN'T THROW STUFF LIKE THAT IN AND NOT EXPLAIN IT.<br /><br />- I ONLY READ THIS BOOK LOOKING FOR A TEEN PREGNANCY. YOU'RE DOING IT RAW EVERY FOUR PAGES AND THEN MAKE IT DIFFICULT TO CONCEIVE? HOW CAN YOU DO THIS TO ME?! WHAT A COP OUT! IF YOU'RE SUCH AN EXPERT ON RELATIONSHIPS, MENTAL HEALTH, AND MEN, WHY DON'T YOU DO SOME MORE BUZZFEED RESEARCH AND BECOME A PREGNANCY EXPERT SO THAT I CAN AT LEAST READ SOMETHING SO RIDICULOUS IT'S HILARIOUS? YOU'RE THE WORST. THE MISCARRIAGE? GLOSSING OVER THAT? REALLY? AND THEN SHE JUST GETS PREGNANT SO EASILY AND THAT'S THAT I CANNOT! <br /><br />- WHY DID YOU PACE THESE BOOKS HORRIBLY FROM START TO FINISH? YOU DRAG EVERYTHING OUT FOR BOOKS AND BOOKS AND THEN #JOKES LET'S JUST SPEED THROUGH THEIR RIDICULOUS LIFE TOGETHER - WHICH YOU SHOULD HAVE DONE IN THE FIRST PLACE.<br /><br />- WHY IS PAPA HARDIN WEARING TIGHT BLACK JEANS - AS A DAD?<br /><br />- WHY DID YOU HAVE TO RUIN THE NAME EMERY FOR ME?<br /><br />- WHY DID THE WHOLE WEDDING/MARRIAGE THING TAKE SO LONG? YOU LITERALLY DON'T KNOW HOW TO WRITE A COMPELLING NOVEL AT ALL.<br /><br />I'm just exhausted with these books and so happy it's over. </span>
  <a data-text-id="4441767212477269541" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText1608507775454364488" style="display:none">4/5 stars.<br />So I finally made my way to the last book, and I managed to give this crazy couple its end. <br />The first three books got from me five big stars, because no matter how stupid Hardin and Tessa behaved, the chemistry was always strong and the plot made me keep reading and reading. I'm not tired of them, and I guess the proof of that is that I read this series 4 times. <br />But somehow... I never managed to start reading the last book. Idk, maybe I was just afraid to break up with this couple, that I learned to love so much.<br />Anyway, I was expecting more from this book. It felt like towards the end, Anna Todd was just trying to finish writing it as fast as possible... The time jumps annoyed me. But despite everything, I was so happy for this couple who managed to get their good ending.</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Elyse  Walters" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Elyse  Walters" href="/user/show/597461-elyse-walters">Elyse  Walters</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2810697139" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11607472951530399986">Audiobook... Hoopla has these books. <br/><br/>“After Ever Happy”, ... book 4....is the best of the series.....<br/>which picked up right where book 3 - “After We Fell”, left off. A satisfying conclusion - but not until we take a different train ride from the first three books. <br/><br/>I can’t believe I read all 4 of these books....<br/>Book 2 - “After We Collided”, is the weakest.<br/><br/>Finished this one yesterday during a walk of 8 miles. <br/><br/>One of the themes that stands out for me was: <br/>“Life is Ok....vs. Life is deeply exhilarati</span>
  <span id="freeText11607472951530399986" style="display:none">Audiobook... Hoopla has these books. <br /><br />“After Ever Happy”, ... book 4....is the best of the series.....<br />which picked up right where book 3 - “After We Fell”, left off. A satisfying conclusion - but not until we take a different train ride from the first three books. <br /><br />I can’t believe I read all 4 of these books....<br />Book 2 - “After We Collided”, is the weakest.<br /><br />Finished this one yesterday during a walk of 8 miles. <br /><br />One of the themes that stands out for me was: <br />“Life is Ok....vs. Life is deeply exhilarating be satisfying”. <br /><br />I think most of us become satisfied- can function with - life being ok. <br />Experiencing deep satisfaction and joy ... the kind of happiness that feels aligned - or beyond our ideal dreams is more rare. <br />Some of us have golden treasure memories of specific times - maybe even<br />lasting a few years— HIGH ON LOVE AND LIFE....( having nothing to do with material things or fancy vacations).., but out of this world inner joy...<br />I think that’s much harder to sustain. <br /><br />But... how many people dare fight for their own deep happiness? Especially as they age?<br />Or is more that we become skillful at things are ok? <br /><br />I’ll never recommend these books to my very mature intelligent adult friends... but I enjoyed the escape — the audiobook doing its thing - side by side - while I did my things....<br />walks, laundry, cleaning, cooking, pool soaking, or sauna listening... <br />I just enjoyed my private time with in Hardin and Tessa’s world. <br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /></span>

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">

<div id="review_1092927490" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1092927490" />
    <a title="Ursula Uriarte" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16751097-ursula-uriarte"><img alt="Ursula Uriarte" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1467336518p2/16751097.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1092927490?book_show_action=true">Oct 30, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ursula Uriarte" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ursula Uriarte" href="/user/show/16751097-ursula-uriarte">Ursula Uriarte</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16751097-ursula-uriarte?shelf=2015">2015</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1092927490" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13843240876273450710">All The Stars!!! <br/><br/>And so the series reaches it’s final stretch and it was a very anticipated (and much dreaded) one, I struggled with dying to know what would happen in the end and not wanting this to be over. Even as I write this review, 2 weeks after having finished reading After Ever Happy, I miss Tessa and Hardin like the day I turned the last page. <br/><br/>First things first, this review has spoilers for the first three books but I will avoid anything spoilery for the last book because everyone dese</span>
  <span id="freeText13843240876273450710" style="display:none">All The Stars!!! <br><br>And so the series reaches it’s final stretch and it was a very anticipated (and much dreaded) one, I struggled with dying to know what would happen in the end and not wanting this to be over. Even as I write this review, 2 weeks after having finished reading After Ever Happy, I miss Tessa and Hardin like the day I turned the last page. <br><br>First things first, this review has spoilers for the first three books but I will avoid anything spoilery for the last book because everyone deserves to suffer… errr I mean experience this book first hand like I did. <br><br>You can check out my reviews for the previous 3 books in the series in the following links: <br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1083143923?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">After</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1090510702?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">After We Collided</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1090510578?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">After We Fell</a><br><br>I don’t even know where to start guys, even thinking about putting down my thoughts and feelings about this book makes my eyes fill up with tears.<br><a href="http://s30.photobucket.com/user/Ursula_Uriarte/media/emotional%20rollercoaster%20gif_zpskxuwvwgk.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424322049ra/13746210.gif" alt=" photo emotional rollercoaster gif_zpskxuwvwgk.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>From the moment this book landed on my doorstep I knew I was officially checking out until I was finished reading.<br><a href="http://s30.photobucket.com/user/Ursula_Uriarte/media/tumblr_m592dt1RBP1ry1wd5o1_500_zpsij7jq95j.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424322278ra/13746252.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m592dt1RBP1ry1wd5o1_500_zpsij7jq95j.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>I think all in all I got about 4 hours of sleep in the span of 62 hours. <br><br>We left off in England, where Trish and Mike are about to get married and Hardin not only walks right into Vance reacquainting himself with Trish but stumbles also into a huge family secret that changes his entire life and shutters the bit of trust he had on others. The news gives him that last push over the edge. <br><a href="http://s30.photobucket.com/user/Ursula_Uriarte/media/tumblr_mzb4bnCEDy1qlrsi6o1_500_zpsfq3v4lck.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424323058ra/13746382.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mzb4bnCEDy1qlrsi6o1_500_zpsfq3v4lck.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>My next thoughts were naturally, Tessa is with Hardin in England and even through this devastation she will be his rock. He will find solace in her. After all, he has been doing so good in controlling his anger and thinking before acting... But then again we are talking Hardin here, why would he ever do what's expected or what makes sense... What transpires in the pages after Vance's big revelation left me literally shaking in what I can only call total and utter disbelief and anger. <br>I went through several stages at this point. My first reaction was wanting to punch Hardin repeatedly, because I just couldn't believe he was being so stupid and cruel! How could he be so cruel!?<br><a href="http://s30.photobucket.com/user/Ursula_Uriarte/media/dean_punching_supernatural_zpskbwrgfft.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424323737ra/13746441.gif" alt=" photo dean_punching_supernatural_zpskbwrgfft.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Tessa can be infuriating at times and I swear she sometimes makes choices that you can't help but think she is purposely testing Hardin's limits but she didn't deserve to have, once again, her heart ripped out of her chest and stomped all over.<br><a href="http://s30.photobucket.com/user/Ursula_Uriarte/media/tumblr_inline_nga5pfoYeS1qcvv5j_zpsxawvso5z.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424324120ra/13746480.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_inline_nga5pfoYeS1qcvv5j_zpsxawvso5z.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>At this point, I couldn't comprehend what was happening, I seriously had to take a break to regroup. <br><a href="http://s30.photobucket.com/user/Ursula_Uriarte/media/tumblr_inline_n7nxjv4Xbm1qd7ceg_zps16qneox0.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424324120ra/13746481.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_inline_n7nxjv4Xbm1qd7ceg_zps16qneox0.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"When you love people, you don't let them destroy you along with themselves, you don't allow them to drag you through the mud. You try to help them, you try to save them, but the moment that your love is one sided or selfish, if you keep on trying, you are a fool. If I loved him, I wouldn't let him ruin me too."</b>
    <i></i>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>When Tessa heads back to Washington, I felt completely empty and lost, I don't think I was even angry anymore, I was numb. My heart was broken into tiny little pieces and once again I felt there was little that could be done to mend things. People have their limits and love and trust can only be pushed so far before it breaks permanently. <br><a href="http://s30.photobucket.com/user/Ursula_Uriarte/media/rain%20gif_zpseyopiwj6.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424325926ra/13746770.gif" alt=" photo rain gif_zpseyopiwj6.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Things go from bad to worse for both Tess and Hardin. Hardin sees, a little too late, that this path of self-loathing and self-sabotaging is not only wrong but unfair, because it hurts the people who love him. <br>It takes terrible circumstances for Hardin to snap out of his stupidity and try to go get the girl he loves, but sadly this time Tessa may really be done with the back and forth with Hardin. <br><a href="http://s30.photobucket.com/user/Ursula_Uriarte/media/prettylittleliarss01e20_zpsw1a0wnbc.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424325926ra/13746771.gif" alt=" photo prettylittleliarss01e20_zpsw1a0wnbc.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>My worst fear coming true and I was almost breaking. The moment they would realize that they were just not good for each other had haunted me from book 1, and everything seemed to be going that direction.<br><br><a href="http://s30.photobucket.com/user/Ursula_Uriarte/media/tumblr_m6aeprWNdG1qcik0wo1_500_zps8snbrae1.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424329400ra/13747346.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m6aeprWNdG1qcik0wo1_500_zps8snbrae1.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br><a href="http://s30.photobucket.com/user/Ursula_Uriarte/media/HESSA_zpsuisbfcae.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424330514ra/13747595.gif" alt=" photo HESSA_zpsuisbfcae.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s30.photobucket.com/user/Ursula_Uriarte/media/tumblr_mmz7iueYK71r5ndk1o1_500_zpstbkioeyb.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424327748ra/13747125.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mmz7iueYK71r5ndk1o1_500_zpstbkioeyb.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>and my answer was always NO! I don't know how that feels but yet I was experiencing it as what felt first hand and I just couldn't stop crying, my cheeks were tear stricken the whole time and I think I have warped the pages on my book. <br><a href="http://s30.photobucket.com/user/Ursula_Uriarte/media/vCAqU78_zpsubnoypqs.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424327748ra/13747126.gif" alt=" photo vCAqU78_zpsubnoypqs.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I would love to go into more detail about the conclusion of this series and the end of the book but I feel that if I did I would be cheating you of experiencing one of the most emotional endings I have ever read in a series. <br>What I can tell you though is that the anguish and complete wreck of emotions never lets go it goes on til the very last page. <br>I couldn't believe Anna was doing this to my heart, I thought I wouldn't make it to the end. <br><a href="http://s30.photobucket.com/user/Ursula_Uriarte/media/elena_zpso7n7evza.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424328013ra/13747156.gif" alt=" photo elena_zpso7n7evza.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So much growth for both Tessa and Hardin. It took them going through so much pain to get through the issues they had with themselves, even if it may have ended up costing them their relationship. <br><br><a href="http://s30.photobucket.com/user/Ursula_Uriarte/media/HARDIN_zps3jbkqlo6.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424330514ra/13747596.gif" alt=" photo HARDIN_zps3jbkqlo6.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://s30.photobucket.com/user/Ursula_Uriarte/media/tumblr_lnmnuhTlDy1qczjlgo1_500_zps8dyucaag.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424329400ra/13747347.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_lnmnuhTlDy1qczjlgo1_500_zps8dyucaag.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Whether Tessa and Hardin end up together in the end...well that's for you to find out. I personally walked into this book with doubts as to whether that would be the case, and what I can say is that I was happy with the way Anna wrapped things up, it was real and it made you think and value what they once had and what it became throughout the course of all 4 books. I think Anna took chances when she wrote the end and for that I thank her because I don't think After will leave me any time soon. <br>I have the hugest series hangover ever, the last one I had was when I finished reading The Infernal Devices, funny I would suffer two major hangovers at the hands of a Tessa. <br>I was out of commission the next day while I processed my feelings. <br><a href="http://s30.photobucket.com/user/Ursula_Uriarte/media/13596412242027637346_zpsvgfk1gpl.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424329400ra/13747348.gif" alt=" photo 13596412242027637346_zpsvgfk1gpl.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>It was worth every single tear shed, every minute spent cursing Hardin out, every single frustrated text to my besties, and every single minute waiting between books! <br><br>Thanks again to Simon and Schuster and Gallery Books for the review copy and thank you Anna for bringing this series to us, it truly was a wonderful roller coaster of feels that I will soon revisit and will never forget. <br><br>After Ever Happy release on February 24th, make sure you pre-order your copy!</span>
  <a data-text-id="13843240876273450710" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2791284255" />

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2791284255?book_show_action=true">Apr 19, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ꮗ€♫◗☿ ❤️ ilikebooksbest.com ❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ꮗ€♫◗☿ ❤️ ilikebooksbest.com ❤️" href="/user/show/70316517-ilikebooksbest-com">Ꮗ€♫◗☿ ❤️ ilikebooksbest.com ❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/23665391-after-ever-happy">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/70316517-ilikebooksbest-com?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/70316517-ilikebooksbest-com?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/70316517-ilikebooksbest-com?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2791284255" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8472037870071657947"><strong>Surprising!</strong><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1579224225ra/28791037.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I liked the ending. I almost never like it when a book goes into the future and shows the couple five or more years down the line, but in this case I really enjoyed the afterward that showed how Hardin and Tessa ended up.<br/><br/>I didn’t really like the middle of the book which I thought wasn’t very realistic given their relationship. I can see Tessa going to New York and getting away from Hardin for a while to be independent and learn to be on her own a bit after some of the things he did to</span>
  <span id="freeText8472037870071657947" style="display:none"><strong>Surprising!</strong><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1579224225ra/28791037.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I liked the ending. I almost never like it when a book goes into the future and shows the couple five or more years down the line, but in this case I really enjoyed the afterward that showed how Hardin and Tessa ended up.<br><br>I didn’t really like the middle of the book which I thought wasn’t very realistic given their relationship. I can see Tessa going to New York and getting away from Hardin for a while to be independent and learn to be on her own a bit after some of the things he did to her. Even though he had stepped up and improved himself so much since then and showed so much growth in handling volatile situations, I could still see her reasons.<br><br>But their love is so tragic and epic and consuming, that I expected things to work out differently than they did. Since when did Tessa start caring what people thought? She was with Hardin from the beginning knowing that people thought he was just using her and he didn’t date. And Tessa came out smelling like a rose for pulling him out of the gutter. Overall I liked the book and it is a good wrap up to the series.<br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> this is what you do when you love someone: you fight for him—you chase after him when you know he needs you. You help him fight the battle against himself, and you never give up on him, even when he gives up on himself.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><br>And whooohoo! No screaming cliffhanger! <br><br><a href="https://www.ilikebooksbest.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a>|<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/wennel" rel="nofollow noopener">Goodreads</a>|<a href="https://www.facebook.com/ilikebooksbest" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a>|<a href="https://www.instagram.com/ilikebooksbest" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a>|<a href="https://www.twitter.com/wendysu020202" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a>|<a href="https://www.bookbub.com/profile/1895823057" rel="nofollow noopener">BookBub</a></span>

<div id="review_3636379194" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3636379194" />
    <a title="Nilufer Ozmekik" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/53701594-nilufer-ozmekik"><img alt="Nilufer Ozmekik" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1559807601p2/53701594.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3636379194?book_show_action=true">Nov 10, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nilufer Ozmekik" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nilufer Ozmekik" href="/user/show/53701594-nilufer-ozmekik">Nilufer Ozmekik</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3636379194" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10304674213913359190">Here I am! Finishing history’s one of the toxic, dysfunctional, passionate, hopeless but interestingly inseparable, devoted couple and their push-pull, extremely angsty, destructive, intense love story! <br/><br/>I thought after all they went through: their story could be ended with a murder! Happy ending doesn’t seem like on the cards for them! <br/><br/>I have to confess, I was planning to skip this series at first. I looked at the long page numbers and I found it too long for YA romance series but eventually I g</span>
  <span id="freeText10304674213913359190" style="display:none">Here I am! Finishing history’s one of the toxic, dysfunctional, passionate, hopeless but interestingly inseparable, devoted couple and their push-pull, extremely angsty, destructive, intense love story! <br /><br />I thought after all they went through: their story could be ended with a murder! Happy ending doesn’t seem like on the cards for them! <br /><br />I have to confess, I was planning to skip this series at first. I looked at the long page numbers and I found it too long for YA romance series but eventually I got bored and watched the first movie on Netflix and the second one on Amazon. Casting was horrible instead of Charlie Weber as Christian Vance ( I adore him as an addicted How to get away with murder fan) But interestingly I got curious what will happen to those characters and who will kill each other first! ( my vote is for Tessa! She has all the vindictive potential and bitchy powers) <br /><br />I couldn’t wait the upcoming movies which will be probably worse than first two. So I bought the last two books, popcorn, red wine, entering the toxicology zone of annoying couple! <br /><br />Yeap, the facts didn’t change: Hardin is still selfish, arrogant, abusive douchebag! And Tessa is not bright, sunshine and flowers girl. Her inner bitch and jealousy slowly replaces with sweet girl next door and she turns into more annoying doormat at each chapter. <br /><br />Third book has the same formula with the previous ones: Hardin makes a dicky move. Tessa gets mad. And Hardin comes back, showing his di*k and Tessa forgives her! <br /><br />So I wanted to skip writing a review for third one which will probably unpopular review and the fans of couple will want to crucify me! No thanks, Holly nails will not suit my outfit. <br /><br /> But I have to admit: I liked the fourth book. Yes! I truly did! At the beginning there were still angsty, irritating, oh no he cannot go that far , wow he actually did moments! Hardin classically made his dickiest move and won the worst detesting human waste award! And finally Tessa gave up after ten thousand dicky moves later! She realizes a man who cannot want to be saved, is doomed to go to hell! <br /><br />And a terrible tragedy shakes her to the core! But interestingly both characters act like they just get illuminated after this big tragedy! They start to act like normal romance couple, more mature to start a conversation! Hardin acted like he’d removed his extra douche characteristics with a surgery and Tessa stopped being self destructive cry baby and wore big girl pants to see how her life would be without Hardin. <br /><br />I wish Hardin could grovel for years like Florentino Ariza who was waiting for his love of his life for 50 years on Love in the time of Cholera! Yeap, I think douchebag never deserves a girl like Tessa but unfortunately she loves him so much and I’m addicted to the HEAs! <br /><br />And I liked the conclusion of the story. Not only for couple Tardin but also for the other characters who found their own HEAs! <br /><br />I know I will passionately hate the adaptation of last book so I advise you to read the book or forget the entire installment.<br /><br />I’m giving my four finally finished and the characters gathered their senses not to act like spoiled brats stars! And getting out of here, singing “I’m addicted to you, that you know you’re toxic?”! Well said Britney!</span>
  <a data-text-id="10304674213913359190" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13658792702160201646"><b>“After everything, we made it. Whatever the hell our souls are made of, they are the same.”</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1551356826i/27130099._SX540_.jpg' width='355' height='270' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I can't believe it's over! Hessa's journey to the happy ending was way too long, passionate, sometimes painful and other times happy. I got to love Hardin and Tessa (especially Hardin), and the supporting characters too (Landon, Karen, Ken, etc...), but also there are some characters I hated (I hated Steph the most). <br/>Things weren't easier in this book either, actually I was a little mad at Tessa, because s</span>

Hessa's journey to the happy ending was way too long, passionate, sometimes painful and other times happy. I did not like that! But beside that this book was a good closure to their love story. <br><br>P.S. I want to talk about One Direction, because this whole story started out as a 1D fanfiction. Honestly I never heard of these books before it was made into a movie, but I'm not gonna lie I used to liked 1D, but they better off solo in my opinion, and actually I prefer Zayn over Harry. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1551356826ra/27130098.gif" width="380" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_2795901351" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2795901351" />
    <a title="Sam" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/48777181-sam"><img alt="Sam" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1551048001p2/48777181.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2795901351?book_show_action=true">Apr 23, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sam" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sam" href="/user/show/48777181-sam">Sam</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2795901351" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8414080638564905265">What a train wreck of a series. What a train wreck of a relationship. <br/><br/><i>“When you love people, you don’t let them destroy you along with themselves, you don’t allow them to drag you through the mud. You try to help them, try to save them, but the moment that your love is one-sided or selfish, if you keep trying, you are a fool.”</i><br/><br/>Tessa, you said this and Tessa you are a fool. <br/><br/>I hate the romanticisation of abusive relationships and I hate that they ended up together. <br/><br/>Anna does a good job of writing a</span>
  <span id="freeText8414080638564905265" style="display:none">What a train wreck of a series. What a train wreck of a relationship. <br /><br /><i>“When you love people, you don’t let them destroy you along with themselves, you don’t allow them to drag you through the mud. You try to help them, try to save them, but the moment that your love is one-sided or selfish, if you keep trying, you are a fool.”</i><br /><br />Tessa, you said this and Tessa you are a fool. <br /><br />I hate the romanticisation of abusive relationships and I hate that they ended up together. <br /><br />Anna does a good job of writing a female who has been sucked in by an abusive, narcissistic sociopath to the point that they question their own behaviour and feel like they’re the problem. I would have loved this book to have had Tessa actually be recommended therapy and have gone to therapy to be able to leave this abusive clusterfuck of a relationship and hightail it out of there and not eventually go back to Hardin. <br /><br />Also, of course Zed had to be made into a bad guy with only one thing on his mind. But that’s only okay for a character to be if his name is Hardin. <br /><br />Moral of the story: give up everything for an abusive POS so he can have you (and your dreams) just so you can have him. <br /><br /><i> “I’m sorry that I couldn’t fix you,” I tell him while softly stroking his damp hair.<br />“Me, too,” he cries against my legs.”</i><br /><br /><b>it is never your job to fix someone. the only person you should feel responsible to heal is yourself</b><br /><br />Harry Styles deserves better. <br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.rainn.org">www.rainn.org</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="8414080638564905265" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1678997986" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer3354650399187493178">I can't believe it's over. I feel like I have been reading about Tessa and Hardin forever, even though it's only been less than two weeks. I was completely sucked into this series from the start. I didn't expect to like it as much as I did based on the reviews and the fact that is fan fiction. Imagine my surprise when I couldn't stop thinking about these characters even after I would put the books down. Every time I got my hands on a new one, I completely devoured it. There was a ton of drama an</span>
  <span id="freeText3354650399187493178" style="display:none">I can't believe it's over. I feel like I have been reading about Tessa and Hardin forever, even though it's only been less than two weeks. I was completely sucked into this series from the start. I didn't expect to like it as much as I did based on the reviews and the fact that is fan fiction. Imagine my surprise when I couldn't stop thinking about these characters even after I would put the books down. Every time I got my hands on a new one, I completely devoured it. There was a ton of drama and back and forth. The relationship is messed up in so many ways just like so many reviews told me it would be. That was kind of the point though. This was a love story of two messed up, imperfect people. It was their passionate and crazy journey. Eventually, they become better people for themselves and for each other. I could never quite give all of the books 5 stars, but not because of my enjoyment. I enjoyed them enough to give them ten stars. I still feel like I may rerate them in the future. I was just very aware of how crazy and destructive the relationship I was reading was, I guess. I rated them the best I could at the time. The books were so long, and so much would happen in each one. I really felt like I was experiencing all the many emotions along with them. I wish I still had many books to read about Tessa and Hardin. I'm so glad I took a chance on this series.</span>
